  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ff3dc0ab-6fa9-449e-892d-14b0e00eb488'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer17456414399773681004">"أجلس اليوم إلى جوارك، أندب أحلامي الحمقى.. غارقة في حبي لك ولا قدرة لي على انتشال بقايا أحلامي من بين حطامك.."، "أحببتك أكثر مما ينبغي، وأحببتني أقل مما أستحق!"<br/>تبدأ الكاتبة السعودية روايتها بنفس المقطع الذي تنتهي به، لتروي بينهما قصة "جمانة" و"عزيز" التي "لن تنتهي!".<br/><br/>تبوح المرأة بتفاصيل مشاعرها تجاه الرجل الذي تحب، والأهم أنها تحاول التعبير عن حالتها الذهنية في تناقضها الح</span>
  <span id="freeText17456414399773681004" style="display:none">"أجلس اليوم إلى جوارك، أندب أحلامي الحمقى.. غارقة في حبي لك ولا قدرة لي على انتشال بقايا أحلامي من بين حطامك.."، "أحببتك أكثر مما ينبغي، وأحببتني أقل مما أستحق!"<br />تبدأ الكاتبة السعودية روايتها بنفس المقطع الذي تنتهي به، لتروي بينهما قصة "جمانة" و"عزيز" التي "لن تنتهي!".<br /><br />تبوح المرأة بتفاصيل مشاعرها تجاه الرجل الذي تحب، والأهم أنها تحاول التعبير عن حالتها الذهنية في تناقضها الحتمي مع حالة الحب الذي تكنّ. فالشرخ الذي يولّد عذابات جمة لا دواء لها، لا بد قائم بين عقلها وقوة مشاعرها، وعطائها الذي لا حدود له للمحبوب: "كنت على استعداد لأن أصغر فتكبر..لأن أفشل لتنجح، لأن أخبو لتلمع.."، ونوعية حبها الذي لا يقدره بل يتجاهله أو يقوم باستغلاله لصالح أهداف أقل أهمية منه بكثير، وأقل قيمة. "ما زلت لا أدرك، لا أدرك كيف يتلاعب رجل بامرأة تحبه من دون أن يخاف للحظة مما يفعله نحوها!"<br /><br />في كل مرة و"بعد كل خيبة أمل.. بعد كل محنة وكل نزوة.. كنت أحاول لملمة أجزائي لنفتح مجدداً صفحة بيضاء أخرى.."، لكن "البدايات الجديدة ما هي إلا كذبة".<br /><br />تستعيد الكاتبة ذكرياتها معه منذ البداية في مقهى خارج الوطن الذي غادرته للدراسة: "الوطن الذي لو لم أغادره لما حدث كل هذا.. أتكون أنت عقابي على مغادرة وطن أحبني!.."، وفكرة العقاب والثواب التي يسخر منها عزيز، تؤمن هي بها: "مؤمنة أنا بيوم الحساب أكثر من أي شيء،" لأنها تأمل عبرها أن ينال عزيز عقابه على ما اقترفه بحقها.<br /><br />قالت لهما العجوز الهندية غريبة الأطوار، دون سابق معرفة: "هي متعبة منك..منك فقط..وأنت متعب من كل شيء.."، وقالت لها "هيفاء" صديقتها الكويتية التي تتخاصم دائما وعزيز، بأنه لا يستحقها، وتقول جمانة له اليوم "حبي لك كان أعمى يا عزيز..وأن هيفاء رأت فيك ما لم أره.."، رأت الكذب المتسلسل والخيانة والإنكار الذي يشكك الآخر بنفسه وبعقله وإحساسه، وهي صفات تتجاهلها المرأة التي تحب رجلاً يحبها لكنه غير قادر على الالتزام بها. قال لها بصراحة: "اسمعي.. أنا رجل لعوب.. أشرب وأعربد وأعاشر النساء.. لكنني أعود إليك في كل مرة.."، وكانت تتحمل الأذى: "تؤذينني عمداً وكأنك تفرغ في نفسي أحقادك وأوجاعك وأمراضك، تؤذيني عمداً باسم الحبّ..". وهي بالرغم من كل الحقائق والوقائع تعترف: "لم أبكِ بحرقة إلا بسببك ولم أضحك من أعماقي إلا معك.. أليست بمعادلة صعبة..؟ يحلل لها زياد صديقهما المشترك الوضع: "أحببته لدرجة أخافته!.. لم يكن قادراً على ضمك لقائمة نسائه ولم يتمكن من الابتعاد عنك.. أحبك لدرجة أنه كان يخشى عليك من نفسه.. كما كان يخشى منك في الوقت ذاته.."<br /><br />كيف يلتقيان، وهو يؤمن بأن الغاية تبرر الوسيلة، وهي تؤمن "بأن الوسيلة أحياناً أهم من الغاية!"؟<br /><br />"قلت لي يوماً بأن حكايات الحبّ الشرقية غالباً ما تنتهي بمأساة. واليوم أعرف بأنك كنت محقاً في هذا.."<br /><br />تنقل الرواية بصدق عميق ما يدور في أعماق المرأة في حالة حب،ّ من أحاسيس وأفكار وتناقضات، إذ تظن أن الخيار الصعب إلى أقسى مداه يكمن في الحفاظ على مشاعر الحبّ الجياشة واستمرارها، على حساب التنكّر للذات الواعية والمدركة لتلاعب الطرف الآخر بها، لكنها بأي حال، وحتى في حال دفع الحساب، لن تحصل على مبتغاها.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17456414399773681004" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer211728291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer75036720851541222">All what I can say about it, is that it is extremely bad one. Honestly, I believe that I could myself have written a story like this some years ago when I was thinking that I might be a writer. This is very bad for many reason. It has no serious events or excitements. It mainly about one theme which is how the girl is deeply attached to that man. She is attached to him to a very great extent that she has canceled her mind totally when it comes to him. But what attracts me to this story many thin</span>
  <span id="freeText75036720851541222" style="display:none">All what I can say about it, is that it is extremely bad one. Honestly, I believe that I could myself have written a story like this some years ago when I was thinking that I might be a writer. This is very bad for many reason. It has no serious events or excitements. It mainly about one theme which is how the girl is deeply attached to that man. She is attached to him to a very great extent that she has canceled her mind totally when it comes to him. But what attracts me to this story many things that I was expecting some issues to be addressed in it but I definitely got disappointed. I have always wondered about something that happened to some friends. A girl can reach to a point when her feelings completely control her. These feelings will shut up all her rational reasoning abilities. So she couldn't think any more. She is always driven by this overwhelming feelings that control her. I always wondered why this would happen. Also how this can be prevented. I also wondered if there are no other feelings that can protect girls at this stage like the feeling of insecurity. Since her mind has stopped working another feelings can do the job and protect her from harmful relationship. Also can a girl be that emotionally susceptible to an extent that make her accept humiliation and lose her dignity as described in the story. Also how all these things can be related to our religion regulations. If the girl is more pious she will be less prone to this situation. This story has disappointed me by all possible means. May god protect all girls</span>
  <a data-text-id="75036720851541222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2363049153" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2363049153" />
    <a title="Lubna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26686119-lubna"><img alt="Lubna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573418272p2/26686119.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2363049153?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lubna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lubna" href="/user/show/26686119-lubna">Lubna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2363049153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3683053869444071945">I appreciate the effort the author put into this novel, but I find it a little bit problematic and understandable how it is considered one of the top books in the Arab region. The book I have is the 21st edition!! ... <br/><br/>The novel is seen from the point of view of "Joumana", a Saudi student studying in Canada who falls in love with "Aziz", also a Saudi student living in Canada for over 10 years. Joumana is telling us about her relation with Aziz and the ups and downs (which are much more than the u</span>
  <span id="freeText3683053869444071945" style="display:none">I appreciate the effort the author put into this novel, but I find it a little bit problematic and understandable how it is considered one of the top books in the Arab region. The book I have is the 21st edition!! ... <br /><br />The novel is seen from the point of view of "Joumana", a Saudi student studying in Canada who falls in love with "Aziz", also a Saudi student living in Canada for over 10 years. Joumana is telling us about her relation with Aziz and the ups and downs (which are much more than the ups) they went through together. <br /><br />The word usage is not strong, the author uses a lot of colloquial language so it is a light easy to read book. I managed to finish it in two days. However, many parts were repetitive and the character sounds extremely weak throughout the novel which personally bothered me. I have been through many relationships and currently in a complicated one and I do understand and realize the pain that comes with intimate relations, but at some point, we reach a place where we cannot be that submissive and weak....or maybe this is my personal idea.<br /><br />I was hoping to find a capturing way to learn how to deal and behave in a complicated relations, but I did not find this in the novel. On the contrary, it made me realize how strong I am regarding my own issues. <br /><br />I will be reading "Fal Taghfuri", which is said that it discusses the relation from Aziz's point of view, just to see what pushes someone to go as far as he did overtime only to go back to his ways.<br /><br />Unfortunately the novel won't get more than 3 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3683053869444071945" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1124935415" />
    <a title="Amal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37048483-amal"><img alt="Amal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417501773p2/37048483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1124935415?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amal" href="/user/show/37048483-amal">Amal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37048483-amal?shelf=mine">mine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1124935415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16905989150989769153"><b>
  <u>What i thought about this book :</u>
</b><br/><br/><u>Main story from my point of view :</u><br/><br/>A Girl "<i>Jomana</i>" who falls in love with the bad boy "<i>Azeez</i>".<br/>a very dramatic love story that leads to a lot of incidents which leaves us with a bad ending for the book and a horrible relation ship.<br/><br/><u>Characters :</u><br/><br/>1- "<i>Jomana</i>" :<br/>A weak and pathetic female in front of her man, but a strong and independent one in front of her family.She is the exact opposite of "<i>Azeez</i>" in every way imaginable and still they came together and could never </span>
  <span id="freeText16905989150989769153" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>What i thought about this book :</u>
</b><br /><br /><u>Main story from my point of view :</u><br /><br />A Girl "<i>Jomana</i>" who falls in love with the bad boy "<i>Azeez</i>".<br />a very dramatic love story that leads to a lot of incidents which leaves us with a bad ending for the book and a horrible relation ship.<br /><br /><u>Characters :</u><br /><br />1- "<i>Jomana</i>" :<br />A weak and pathetic female in front of her man, but a strong and independent one in front of her family.She is the exact opposite of "<i>Azeez</i>" in every way imaginable and still they came together and could never part .<br />2- "<i>Azeez</i>" :<br />A lying, cheating and worthless man ,Fooling around and drinking are his greatest ambitions in life. A man who hates his home town "Saudi Arabia" and everything related to it except "<i>Jomana</i>" .The only one that he couldn't treat her the way he treats other women, she was too pure to destroy as she was his weakness.<br /><br /><u>Why it deserved 2 stars out of 5 :</u><br /><br />1- I found both characters irritating in their own way ,<br /><i>Jomana</i> was annoyingly pushy and needy.her life was centered around <i>Azeez</i>,<br /><i>Azeez's</i> character is a abomination , i hate him. When <i>Jomana</i> does something wrong he punishes her by cheating on her and she doesn't even know that he cheats , and when he does he feels like he had done her justice , <i>How sick is that</i> ?<br /><br />2- This book affected me in the worst ways possible, the week i was reading it and its sequel i was seriously depressed.<br /><br />3- <i>Jomana's</i> bleeding and <i>Azeez's</i> stubbornness are realistic compared to our world today, but the writer's style of writing pained me even more than the original story as all i had for <i>Jomana</i> was pity and all i had for <i>Azeez</i> was loathing.<br /><br />4- The author's style is unique and inspiring but it felt like a waste of time and ink on this book .<br /><br />5- Another thing i liked about this book was the quotations in every few pages, i found them interesting and knowledgeable.<br /><br /><br /><br />If you would like to cry your eyes out (not the good kind of crying) or you have a negative build up energy i think you should read that book. if not then DON'T do it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16905989150989769153" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15239522959016053566" style="display:none">Still not over the book tbh, I'm trying to justify Jumana's actions but It's not making sense, how can she love someone who is slowly destroying her, turning her into the mister he is? What she calls "love" in the book doesn't justify the relationship whatsoever, she's way too naive and he's too manipulative. Them being together does not make sense and it never will. Tamam I get it sometimes you fall in love with the wrong person, a person you can never be with, but you just try to forget about them and let your mind/morals be the better judge of the situation. You don't chase someone who isn't right for you and you definitely shouldn't sacrifice for. In my opinion, Jumana was such a weak person she was chasing a pointless dream &amp; kept allowing an asshole to hurt her over and over again. No character development whatsoever, on the contrary her character was becoming more pathetic page after page. </span>

    <a title="Romaissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28522039-romaissa"><img alt="Romaissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509470762p2/28522039.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1922651163?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Romaissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Romaissa" href="/user/show/28522039-romaissa">Romaissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1922651163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6882321768617494517">I always start my reviews with my affection from the book, but i don't know how i feel towards this one. Yet, i'm sure that i'm not going to miss it or want to read it again. <br/>There was so much expressed emotions and little plot in this book. The novel is written from 1st person point of view and the protagonist was more into expressing her feelings than actually narrating the novel, so the plot was not really there. There was also a lot of contradictions in the feelings of the protagonist; once,</span>
  <span id="freeText6882321768617494517" style="display:none">I always start my reviews with my affection from the book, but i don't know how i feel towards this one. Yet, i'm sure that i'm not going to miss it or want to read it again. <br />There was so much expressed emotions and little plot in this book. The novel is written from 1st person point of view and the protagonist was more into expressing her feelings than actually narrating the novel, so the plot was not really there. There was also a lot of contradictions in the feelings of the protagonist; once, she is speaking with bitterness and loathe towards her loved one, because he mistreats her and done some bad things to her. Then, she is speaking with love and passion and saying that he will always be sacred for her, even with his many sins. So she was jumping from these feelings to the others through the whole book and it annoyed me. <br />I couldn't feel any sympathy towards the protagonist as i couldn't hate her loved one for making him seem as a bad guy and there was no characters development.<br />The author kept the ending open (I guess) and it made the novel seems less interesting. Speaking of the author, i read for her before ( في ديسمبر تنتهي كل الاحلام ) and i really liked it, but for this one, i'm not sure i do.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6882321768617494517" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B2PvxbJKmxmGCbrYOIiaea9Q06kVaUBUkG1MiY+dpKrvk4UVbdaAxG5Z3Xksg3hAdpVCtKAX2KIE3UYaHX8rwg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1NYdpBvpw2AZPYqcE7/D4s95RJyYlKdT+NcIBloNMNU8Jnd0xHXYvfFt7T0HtCHbFrzVgS3qP6VsZwKVyO+/vQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

دفعة واحدة من السّماد في ربيع كلّ عام، وتربة رطبة دون فيض من السقيا.\nجميع أنواع الياسمين تفضل النّموّ في مكان مشمس، لكنّها تتحمّل وجود شيء من الظلّ. وشمس تونس كانت مواتية لنضجها وتكوين شخصيّتها، وقد أصبحت جاهزة لتحمّل شيء من ظلالأوروبا ذات المناخ البارد. مثل الياسمين الأبيض المتوسّطي، كانت رقيقة في مظهرها، لكنّ شخصيّتها قويّة وثابتة، مثل رائحة الياسمين النفّاذة والفريدة التي تبثّ إحساسا بالدّفء لا تملكه الورود الأخرى.\nلم تتكلّم عن دلالة الياسمين العاطفيّة التي بحثت ياسمين عنها مذ اهتمّت بمدلولات الزهور في بداية مراهقتها. عرفت أنّ إهداء زهر الياسمين لامرأة يعني “لماذا لا تحبّين أبدًا؟”. والدها أهداها هي، ياسمين، إلى والدتها. كانت آخر عطاياه لها حين تخلّى عن حضانتها إثر الطّلاق. وهي “لم تحبّ بعده أبدًا”. كانت جديرة بتقبّل زهرة الياسمين.\nتفتقد أمها كل يوم أكثر من اليوم الماضي. مع مرور الوقت تزداد يقينًا من ضياعها بدونها. كانت تعلم أن الغربة ليست تجربة سهلة، ومع ذلك وافقت على سفرها. علّمتها كيف تكون ياسمينة حقيقيّة. لكن لعلّها غفلت عن حقيقة مرّة. زهرة الياسمين تذبل بسرعة حين تغادر تربتها وتنسّق في شكل “مشموم” جميل.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"5186525672970647256\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n      <div
